--- Commit Message ---
LU-10018 protocol: MDT as a statfs proxy

MDT can act as a proxy for statfs data. this should
make df faster (RTT vs RTT*(#MDTs+1)) and enable
idling connections so that clients don't connect to
each OST just to report statfs data. the protocol
has been changing slightly to let MDT differentiate
self and aggregated statfs.

also, obd_statfs has got a new field "granted" where
OST reports how much space has been granted to the
requesting MDT so that space can be added to available
space.

client's NID is used to distribute MDS_STATFS among
MDTS.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2017-10-19 11:11:23.000000000) ---
Patch Set 24:

(1 comment)

As for how the clients can distribute themselves among MDTs, this could be done by any number of methods.  Using one of:

  mdt_idx = (client NID, client UUID, (client pointer >> 16)) % MDT_count

as the MDT index to send the STATFS to allows a relatively uniform distribution across MDTs without any pre-arranged secret.

General question: lots of our recovery code assumes that df (lfs df actually) goes to all servers and is used as such as a marker that recovery is done/completed.

I imagine you need to update that too? Or is lfs df unaffected by these changes?

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2018-08-08 11:21:15.000000000) ---
Patch Set 85:

> General question: lots of our recovery code assumes that df (lfs df actually) goes to all servers and is used as such as a marker that recovery is done/completed.

lfs df uses obd_iocontrol() and doesn't pass OBD_STATFS_SUM down the stack, so MDT doesn't  aggregate statfs data and then the client has to talk to each target.
